    Wu=Kc(Wu)
    local z=af()

        local sd=(function(...)
            return{...},Fv('#',...)
        end)
        local nf;
        nf=(function(vf,vo,Rc)
            if vo>Rc then
                return
            end
            return vf[vo],nf(vf,vo+1,Rc)
        end)
        local function Vb(xa,Sm,ro,Pu)
            local za,wb,Ka,Bq,pd,Lg,Lm,Cd,hu,Rt,on,Aq,os,Pi,Lr,qb,xl,xf,Bl,oc,wi,Bj,Jk,ba;

            end;
            on=xf[-8524]or Lm(56139,-8524,18663)
